     $.strRemove = function(theTarget, theString) {
         return $("<div/>").append(
             $(theTarget, theString).remove().end()
         ).html();
     };
 
     var articleStr = sessionStorage.getItem('h5ab-print-article');
     var removeArr = ['video','audio','script','iframe'];
 
     $.each(removeArr, function(index, value){
         var processedCode = $.strRemove(value, articleStr);
         articleStr = processedCode;
     });
     
     var fullPrintContent = articleStr;
     sessionStorage.setItem('h5ab-print-article', fullPrintContent);
     
 });

    <div id="main_content">
     <div class="elementor elementor-4015">
      <div class="elementor-inner">
       <div class="elementor-section-wrap">
        <section class="elementor-element elementor-element-p5rqkbi elementor-section-full_width elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default default-style elementor-section elementor-top-section" data-element_type="section" data-id="p5rqkbi" data-settings='{"rt_color_sets":"default-style"}'>
         <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-no">
          <div class="elementor-row">
           <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-tqq9t7w elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column" data-element_type="column" data-id="tqq9t7w">
            <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
             <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
              <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5vf4vty elementor-widget elementor-widget-rt-slider" data-element_type="rt-slider.default" data-id="5vf4vty">
               <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                <div class="rt-carousel main-carousel carousel-holder clearfix" data-autoplay="true" data-dots="false" data-fullheight="false" data-item-width="1" data-mobile-height="300" data-nav="false" data-parallax="false" data-thumbnails="true" data-timeout="30000" id="content-slider-582660" style="min-height:450px">
                 <div class="rt-carousel-holder" style="min-height:450px">
                  <div class="owl-carousel">
                   <div class="item has-bg-image light-style" data-color-tone="light" style="min-height: 450px;">
                    <a href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/online-patientenverfuegung/" target="_self" title="">
                    </a>
                    <div class="slide-content-wrapper default clearfix" style="min-height: 450px;">
                     <div class="slide-content left text-left" style="width: 51%;">
                      <h2 class="slide_heading" data-maxfont-size="46" data-minfont-size="40" data-mobile-value="28" style="font-size:46px;">
                       Standard Patientenverfügung
                      </h2>
                      <div class="slide-text" data-mobile-value="18" style="">
                       <p>
                        Aktuell: immer auf dem neuesten Stand der Rechtssprechung
                        <br/>
                        Komplett: samt notwendiger Vollmachten
                        <br/>
                        Gültig: auch ohne notarielle Beurkundung
                       </p>
                      </div>
                      <div class="button_wrapper arrow rounded">
                       <a class="button_ white small" href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/online-patientenverfuegung/" target="_self" title="HIER online erstellen">
                        <span>
                         <span>
                          HIER online erstellen
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </a>

     $.strRemove = function(theTarget, theString) {
         return $("<div/>").append(
             $(theTarget, theString).remove().end()
         ).html();
     };
 
     var articleStr = sessionStorage.getItem('h5ab-print-article');
     var removeArr = ['video','audio','script','iframe'];
 
     $.each(removeArr, function(index, value){
         var processedCode = $.strRemove(value, articleStr);
         articleStr = processedCode;
     });
     
     var fullPrintContent = articleStr;
     sessionStorage.setItem('h5ab-print-article', fullPrintContent);

     $.strRemove = function(theTarget, theString) {
         return $("<div/>").append(
             $(theTarget, theString).remove().end()
         ).html();
     };
 
     var articleStr = sessionStorage.getItem('h5ab-print-article');
     var removeArr = ['video','audio','script','iframe'];
 
     $.each(removeArr, function(index, value){
         var processedCode = $.strRemove(value, articleStr);
         articleStr = processedCode;
     });
     
     var fullPrintContent = articleStr;
     sessionStorage.setItem('h5ab-print-article', fullPrintContent);
     
 });

     <div class="elementor elementor-4015">
      <div class="elementor-inner">
       <div class="elementor-section-wrap">
        <section class="elementor-element elementor-element-p5rqkbi elementor-section-full_width elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default default-style elementor-section elementor-top-section" data-element_type="section" data-id="p5rqkbi" data-settings='{"rt_color_sets":"default-style"}'>
         <div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-no">
          <div class="elementor-row">
           <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-tqq9t7w elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column" data-element_type="column" data-id="tqq9t7w">
            <div class="elementor-column-wrap elementor-element-populated">
             <div class="elementor-widget-wrap">
              <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5vf4vty elementor-widget elementor-widget-rt-slider" data-element_type="rt-slider.default" data-id="5vf4vty">
               <div class="elementor-widget-container">
                <div class="rt-carousel main-carousel carousel-holder clearfix" data-autoplay="true" data-dots="false" data-fullheight="false" data-item-width="1" data-mobile-height="300" data-nav="false" data-parallax="false" data-thumbnails="true" data-timeout="30000" id="content-slider-582660" style="min-height:450px">
                 <div class="rt-carousel-holder" style="min-height:450px">
                  <div class="owl-carousel">
                   <div class="item has-bg-image light-style" data-color-tone="light" style="min-height: 450px;">
                    <a href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/online-patientenverfuegung/" target="_self" title="">
                    </a>
                    <div class="slide-content-wrapper default clearfix" style="min-height: 450px;">
                     <div class="slide-content left text-left" style="width: 51%;">
                      <h2 class="slide_heading" data-maxfont-size="46" data-minfont-size="40" data-mobile-value="28" style="font-size:46px;">
                       Standard Patientenverfügung
                      </h2>
                      <div class="slide-text" data-mobile-value="18" style="">
                       <p>
                        Aktuell: immer auf dem neuesten Stand der Rechtssprechung
                        <br/>
                        Komplett: samt notwendiger Vollmachten
                        <br/>
                        Gültig: auch ohne notarielle Beurkundung
                       </p>
                      </div>
                      <div class="button_wrapper arrow rounded">
                       <a class="button_ white small" href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/online-patientenverfuegung/" target="_self" title="HIER online erstellen">
                        <span>
                         <span>
                          HIER online erstellen
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="slide-background" style="background-image: url(https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/483290237.jpg);background-size: cover;background-position: center center;">
                    </div>
                   </div>
                   <div class="item has-bg-image light-style" data-color-tone="light" style="min-height: 450px;">
                    <a href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/optimal-massgeschneiderte-individuelle-patientenverfuegung-opv/" target="_self" title="">
                    </a>
                    <div class="slide-content-wrapper default clearfix" style="min-height: 450px;">
                     <div class="slide-content left" style="width: 51%;">
                      <h2 class="slide_heading" data-maxfont-size="46" data-minfont-size="40" data-mobile-value="28" style="font-size:46px;">
                       Optimale Patientenverfügung
                      </h2>
                      <div class="slide-text" data-mobile-value="18" style="">
                       <p>
                        Differenziert: Erfasst alle Eventualitäten, ohne jegliche Reichweitenbeschränkung
                        <br/>
                        Individuell: Persönliche Wünsche und Vorgaben werden integriert
                        <br/>
                        Bewährt seit über 25 Jahren
                       </p>
                      </div>
                      <div class="button_wrapper arrow rounded">
                       <a class="button_ white small" href="https://2017.patientenverfuegung.de/?p=4651" target="_self" title="HIER zum Fragebogen">
                        <span>
                         <span>
                          HIER zum Fragebogen
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="slide-background" style="background-image: url(https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/522310646.jpg);background-size: cover;background-position: center center;">
                    </div>
                   </div>
                   <div class="item has-bg-image light-style" data-color-tone="light" style="min-height: 450px;">
                    <a href="https://www.patientenverfuegung.de/fuer-den-betreuungsfall-zwei-einander-ergaenzende-vorsorgevollmachten-formulare/" target="_self" title="">
                    </a>
                    <div class="slide-content-wrapper default clearfix" style="min-height: 450px;">
                     <div class="slide-content left text-left" style="width: 51%;">
                      <h2 class="slide_heading" data-maxfont-size="46" data-minfont-size="40" data-mobile-value="28" style="font-size:46px;">
                       Gesundheits- &amp; Vorsorgevollmacht
                      </h2>
                      <div class="slide-text" data-mobile-value="18" style="">
                       <p>
                        Mit den Vorsorge-Dokumenten legen Sie fest, WER für Sie Entscheidungen treffen soll, wenn Sie es nicht mehr können
                       </p>
                      </div>
                      <div class="button_wrapper arrow rounded">

     $.strRemove = function(theTarget, theString) {
         return $("<div/>").append(
             $(theTarget, theString).remove().end()
         ).html();
     };
 
     var articleStr = sessionStorage.getItem('h5ab-print-article');
     var removeArr = ['video','audio','script','iframe'];
 
     $.each(removeArr, function(index, value){
         var processedCode = $.strRemove(value, articleStr);
         articleStr = processedCode;
     });
     
     var fullPrintContent = articleStr;
     sessionStorage.setItem('h5ab-print-article', fullPrintContent);
     
 });
   </script>
